148// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_DIO_IRQ_CONFIG
149#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RX_FIFO (0x01UL << 0) // 31 0 interrupt: Rx FIFO threshold reached
150#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_TX_FIFO (0x01UL << 1) // 31 0 Tx FIFO threshold reached
151#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RNG_REQ_VALID (0x01UL << 2) // 31 0 ranging slave received valid request
152#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_TX_TIMESTAMP (0x01UL << 3) // 31 0 end of packet Tx timestamp
153#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RX_TIMESTAMP (0x01UL << 4) // 31 0 end of packet Rx timestamp
154#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_PREAMBLE_DETECTED (0x01UL << 5) // 31 0 preamble detected
155#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_HEADER_VALID (0x01UL << 6) // 31 0 LoRa header received and valid
156#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_SYNCWORD_VALID (0x01UL << 6) // 31 0 sync word valid
157#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_CAD_DETECTED (0x01UL << 7) // 31 0 channel activity detected
158#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_HDR_TIMESTAMP (0x01UL << 8) // 31 0 LoRa header timestamp
159#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_HDR_CRC_ERROR (0x01UL << 9) // 31 0 LoRa header CRC error
160#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_EOL (0x01UL << 10) // 31 0 end of life
161#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_PA_OCP_OVP (0x01UL << 11) // 31 0 PA overcurrent/overvoltage triggered
162#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_TX_RX_HOP (0x01UL << 12) // 31 0 LoRa intra-packet hopping
163#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_SYNC_FAIL (0x01UL << 13) // 31 0 sync word match detection failed
164#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_SYMBOL_END (0x01UL << 14) // 31 0 symbol end
165#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LORA_TIMESTAMP_STAT (0x01UL << 15) // 31 0 new stats available
166#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_ERROR (0x01UL << 16) // 31 0 error other than command error
167#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_CMD_ERROR (0x01UL << 17) // 31 0 command error
168#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RX_DONE (0x01UL << 18) // 31 0 packet received
169#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_TX_DONE (0x01UL << 19) // 31 0 packet transmitted
170#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_CAD_DONE (0x01UL << 20) // 31 0 CAD finished
171#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_TIMEOUT (0x01UL << 21) // 31 0 Rx or Tx timeout
172#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_CRC_ERROR (0x01UL << 22) // 31 0 CRC error
173#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_LEN_ERROR (0x01UL << 23) // 31 0 length error on received packet
174#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_ADDR_ERROR (0x01UL << 24) // 31 0 packet with incorrect address received
175#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_FHSS (0x01UL << 25) // 31 0 FHSS intra-packet hopping
176#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_INTER_PACKET_FREQ (0x01UL << 26) // 31 0 inter packet hopping can load new frequency table
177#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_INTER_NEW_PAYLOAD (0x01UL << 27) // 31 0 inter packet hopping can load new payload
178#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RNG_RESP_DONE (0x01UL << 28) // 31 0 slave ranging response sent
179#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RNG_REQ_DIS (0x01UL << 29) // 31 0 ranging request discarded
180#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RNG_EXCH_VALID (0x01UL << 30) // 31 0 master receive valid ranging response
181#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_RNG_TIMEOUT (0x01UL << 31) // 31 0 ranging timeout
182#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IRQ_ALL (0xFFFFFFFFUL) // 31 0 all interrupts
183
184// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_SLEEP
185#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SLEEP_32K_CLK_DISABLED (0x00UL << 0) // 0 0 32 kHz clock: disabled
186#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SLEEP_32K_CLK_ENABLED (0x01UL << 0) // 0 0 enabled
187#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SLEEP_RETENTION_DISABLED (0x00UL << 1) // 1 1 configuration retention in sleep mode: disabled
188#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SLEEP_RETENTION_ENABLED (0x01UL << 1) // 1 1 enabled
189
190// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_STANDBY
191#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_STANDBY_RC (0x00UL << 0) // 7 0 standby mode: RC oscillator
192#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_STANDBY_XOSC (0x01UL << 0) // 7 0 XOSC oscillator
193
194// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_RX
195#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_RX_TIMEOUT_NONE (0x000000UL) // 23 0 Rx timeout duration: no timeout (Rx single mode)
196#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_RX_TIMEOUT_INF (0xFFFFFFUL) // 23 0 infinite (Rx continuous mode)
197
198// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_TX
199#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_TX_TIMEOUT_NONE (0x000000UL) // 23 0 disable Tx timeout
200
201// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_RX_TX_FALLBACK_MODE
202#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_FALLBACK_MODE_STBY_RC (0x01UL << 0) // 1 0 fallback mode after Rx/Tx: standby with RC
203#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_FALLBACK_MODE_STBY_XOSC (0x02UL << 0) // 1 0 standby with XOSC
204#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_FALLBACK_MODE_FS (0x03UL << 0) // 1 0 frequency synthesis
205
206// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_RX_DUTY_CYCLE
207#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_RX_DUTY_CYCLE_MODE_RX (0x00UL << 0) // 0 0 mode in Rx windows: Rx (default)
208#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_RX_DUTY_CYCLE_MODE_CAD (0x01UL << 0) // 0 0 CAD
209
210// RADIOLIB_LR20210_CMD_AUTO_TX_RX
211#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AUTO_MODE_NONE (0x00UL << 0) // 1 0 auto rx-tx mode: never enable auto rx-tx
212#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AUTO_MODE_ALWAYS (0x01UL << 0) // 1 0 auto rx-tx on every RxDone or TxDone event
213#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AUTO_MODE_OK (0x02UL << 0) // 1 0 auto rx-tx on valid Rx packet only (Tx always)
214#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AUTO_MODE_CLEAR_DISABLED (0x00UL << 7) // 7 7 automatically disable auto rx-tx on timeout: disabled
215#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AUTO_MODE_CLEAR_ENABLED (0x01UL << 7) // 7 7 enabled
216
217// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_REG_MODE
218#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_SIMO_OFF (0x00UL << 0) // 7 0 SIMO mode: disabled
219#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_SIMO_NORMAL (0x02UL << 0) // 7 0 normal
220#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_RES_2_US (0x00UL << 5) // 6 5 ramp timing resolution: 2 us
221#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_RES_4_US (0x01UL << 5) // 6 5 4 us
222#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_RES_8_US (0x02UL << 5) // 6 5 8 us
223#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_RES_16_US (0x03UL << 5) // 6 5 16 us
224#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_INDEX_RC2RU (0)
225#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_INDEX_TX2RU (1)
226#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_INDEX_RU2RC (2)
227#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_REG_MODE_RAMP_INDEX_RAMP_DOWN (3)
228
229// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_CALIBRATE
230#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_LF_RC (0x01UL << 0) // 0 0 blocks to calibrate: low-frequency RC
231#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_HF_RC (0x01UL << 1) // 1 1 high-frequency RC
232#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_PLL (0x01UL << 2) // 2 2 phase-locked loop
233#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_AAF (0x01UL << 3) // 3 3 anti-aliasing filter
234#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_MU (0x01UL << 5) // 4 4 measurement unit
235#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_PA_OFF (0x01UL << 6) // 5 5 power amplifier offset
236#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_ALL (0x6FUL << 0) // 7 0 everything
237
238// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_CALIB_FRONT_END
239#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_FE_LF_PATH (0x00UL << 15) // 15 15 calibration path: low-frequency
240#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CALIBRATE_FE_HF_PATH (0x01UL << 15) // 15 15 high-frequency
241#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CAL_IMG_FREQ_TRIG_MHZ (20.0f)
242#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_LF_CUTOFF_FREQ (1500.0f)
243
244// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_GET_V_BAT
245#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_VBAT_FORMAT_RAW (0x00UL << 3) // 3 3 readout format: raw
246#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_VBAT_FORMAT_MV (0x01UL << 3) // 3 3 millivolts
247#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_MEAS_RESOLUTION_OFFSET (8)
248
249// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_GET_TEMP
250#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_TEMP_SOURCE_VBE (0x00UL << 4) // 4 4 temperature source: sensor near Vbe junction
251#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_TEMP_SOURCE_XOSC (0x01UL << 4) // 4 4 sensor near XOSC
252#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_TEMP_FORMAT_RAW (0x00UL << 3) // 3 3 readout format: raw
253#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_TEMP_FORMAT_DEG_C (0x01UL << 3) // 3 3 degrees Celsius
254
255// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_SET_EOL_CONFIG
256#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V6 (0x00UL << 1) // 3 1 EoL trigger threshold: 1.60 V
257#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V67 (0x01UL << 1) // 3 1 1.67 V
258#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V74 (0x02UL << 1) // 3 1 1.74 V
259#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V8 (0x03UL << 1) // 3 1 1.80 V
260#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V88 (0x04UL << 1) // 3 1 1.88 V (default)
261#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_1V95 (0x05UL << 1) // 3 1 1.95 V
262#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_2V0 (0x06UL << 1) // 3 1 2.00 V
263#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_EOL_TRIM_2V1 (0x07UL << 1) // 3 1 2.10 V

265// RADIOLIB_LR2021_CMD_GET_ERRORS
266#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_HF_XOSC_START_ERR (0x01UL << 0) // 15 0 error: high-frequency XOSC failed to start
267#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_LF_XOSC_START_ERR (0x01UL << 1) // 15 0 low-frequency XOSC failed to start
268#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_PLL_LOCK_ERR (0x01UL << 2) // 15 0 PLL failed to lock
269#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_LF_RC_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 3) // 15 0 low-frequency RC calibration failed
270#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_HF_RC_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 4) // 15 0 high-frequency RC calibration failed
271#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_PLL_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 5) // 15 0 PLL calibration failed
272#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_AAF_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 6) // 15 0 anti-aliasing filter calibration failed
273#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_IMG_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 7) // 15 0 image rejection calibration failed
274#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_CHIP_BUSY_ERR (0x01UL << 8) // 15 0 Tx or Rx could not be processed because chips was busy
275#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_RXFREQ_NO_FE_CAL_ERR (0x01UL << 9) // 15 0 front-end calibration nto available for this Rx frequency
276#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_MEAS_UNIT_ADC_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 10) // 15 0 measurement unit ADC calibration failed
277#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_PA_OFFSET_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 11) // 15 0 PA offset calibration failed
278#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_PPF_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 12) // 15 0 poly-phase filter calibration failed
279#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SRC_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 13) // 15 0 self-reception cancellation calibration failed
280#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SRC_SATURATION_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 14) // 15 0 RSSI saturation during SRC calibration
281#define RADIOLIB_LR2021_SRC_TOLERANCE_CALIB_ERR (0x01UL << 15) // 15 0 self-reception cancellation values out of tolernce
